<div style="text-align:center"><div style="width:8.5in;text-align:left;margin-left: auto;margin-right: auto">
 <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold">Item&#8201;5.02 Departure of Directors or Principal Officers; Election of Directors; Appointment of Principal Officers. </p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On February&#160;18, 2025, Kelvin Westbrook notified <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> US, Inc. (the &#8220;Company&#8221;) of his decision to not to stand for <span style="white-space:nowrap">re-election</span> to the Board of Directors (the &#8220;Board&#8221;) of the Company at the 2025 Annual Meeting of Stockholders (the &#8220;Annual Meeting&#8221;). Mr.&#160;Westbrook&#8217;s departure from the Board and its Compensation Committee will be effective immediately after the conclusion of the Annual Meeting. Additionally, on February&#160;18, 2025, Srini Gopalan notified the Board of his decision to resign from the Board and its Compensation Committee, effective as of February&#160;28, 2025, due to his acceptance of a new role at the Company as the Company&#8217;s Chief Operating Officer. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Mr.&#160;Westbrook&#8217;s decision not to stand for <span style="white-space:nowrap">re-election</span> and Mr.&#160;Gopalan&#8217;s resignation from the board are not the result of any disagreement between Messrs. Westbrook and Gopalan and the Company on any matters relating to the operations, policies or practices of the Company. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company also announced that the Board intends to nominate Thomas Dannenfeldt to serve as a director to the Board at the 2025 Annual Meeting. Mr.&#160;Dannenfeldt previously served on the Company&#8217;s Board from 2013 to 2018, and was the Chief Financial Officer of Deutsche Telekom AG from 2014 through 2018. Mr.&#160;Dannenfeldt currently serves as Chairman of the board of directors of Ceconomy AG and on the board of directors of Nokia Oyi. </p> <p style="font-size:18pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p>
</div></div>
